<div class="para">八月十五夜<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />当地的年轻人都爱到新婚夫妇家中去再闹&quot;新房&quot;<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />他们拿着丝瓜轻轻地敲打新婚夫妇<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />一边打一边问<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=820013475104505573524673609" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />生儿不生儿<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=539295395257695099998793656" />……<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />直打到新婚夫妇说<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=820013475104505573524673609" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />我俩一定生个大胖儿<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=874273422226782269187107689" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" />为止<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />解放后<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />这种活动渐渐停止<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">猪头插筷子</div>

<div class="para"><b>白雀人之家</b></div><div class="anchor-list"><a name="16" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="sub985021_16" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="" class="anchor-1"></a></div><h2 class="headline-1"><span class="headline-1-index">16</span><span class="headline-content">互联网发展</span><span class="text_edit editable-title" style="margin-left: 10px;" data-edit-id="4795335:%E7%99%BD%E9%9B%80%E5%9B%AD:16"><a href="#" class="nslog:1019" title="编辑本段">编辑</a></span></h2><div class="para">1.2006年12月<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />白雀园人创办<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />白雀人之家论坛<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" /><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />白雀人之家采用phpwind文本论坛<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />目前注册会员达31000多人<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />日在线500人<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />成为白雀园互联网历史上第一个本地论坛社区<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />白雀园刘晓翠<sup>[4]</sup><a class="anchor-inline" name="ref_[4]_985021">&nbsp;</a>于2012年2月正式加入白雀人之家论坛<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />现为论坛第六届管理团队总版主之一<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
